Ask HP Back $999.00 $1799.00 To top Features Buy Back Features HP EliteBook Folio HP EliteBook Folio The world's thinnest and lightest business-class notebook.1 Exquisite craftsmanship and exceptional performance are united in the HP EliteBook Folio. With hand-selected materials and premium features optimized for collaboration, it's the choice for those who value a flawless experience. View all options Elevating durable design Cutting-edge design, innovative engineering, and refined materials come together in the sophisticated and durable HP EliteBook Folio. Equipped to get the job done Be productive in any situation. Windows 10 Pro2 and powerful security, collaboration, and connectivity features from HP help you power through your day on the HP EliteBook Folio. Windows Hello biometric authentication with IR camera HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard Bang & Olufsen audio 12.5 diagonal inch UHD touchscreen3 Dock capable (via USB Type-C™ ports with Thunderbolt™) Premium collaboration Engage teams, clients, and vendors with the crystal-clear audio by Bang & Olufsen and the high-performance HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard that allows you to launch calls and video chats at the touch of a button on the world's first notebook purpose-built for collaboration.4 The solution for diverse business demands Design Elevating exceptional design Weighing less than 2.2 lb/1kg this PC is designed to turn heads with a polished diamond-cut CNC aluminum, durable body. The ultra-thin design features a 180-degree unique piano hinge to lay completely flat for easy sharing with others. Security Deepest level of security New security threats drive the need for new protections. HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection5, exclusively from HP, identifies and fixes BIOS attacks and Windows 10 Pro2 allows multi-factor authentication to help secure access to business networks and resources. IR camera Leave passwords behind. Use Windows Hello biometric authentication with the IR camera to help prevent unauthorized access to business networks and resources with Windows 10 Pro.2 Screens simulate, subject to change; Apps sold separately, availability may vary. Performance Performance to get the job done The HP EliteBook Folio handles high-performance requirements with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processor,6 PCle SSDs, 8GB of memory, and long battery life. Clarity Clear, sharp vivid display Choose a crystal-clear UHD display3 with four times more pixels than FHD displays for color critical applications, or an FHD touch display3 for outstanding visual and touch interactivity. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. It's what professional service and support should be. Standard with every Elite PC, schedule a call today, at 1-866-625-1175. With hand-selected materials and premium features optimized for collaboration, it's the choice for those who value a flawless experience. View all options Elevating durable design Cutting-edge design, innovative engineering, and refined materials come together in the sophisticated and durable HP EliteBook Folio. Equipped to get the job done Be productive in any situation. Windows 10 Pro2 and powerful security, collaboration, and connectivity features from HP help you power through your day on the HP EliteBook Folio. Windows Hello biometric authentication with IR camera HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard Bang & Olufsen audio 12.5 diagonal inch UHD touchscreen3 Dock capable (via USB Type-C™ ports with Thunderbolt™) Premium collaboration Engage teams, clients, and vendors with the crystal-clear audio by Bang & Olufsen and the high-performance HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard that allows you to launch calls and video chats at the touch of a button on the world's first notebook purpose-built for collaboration.4 The solution for diverse business demands Design Elevating exceptional design Weighing less than 2.2 lb/1kg this PC is designed to turn heads with a polished diamond-cut CNC aluminum, durable body. The ultra-thin design features a 180-degree unique piano hinge to lay completely flat for easy sharing with others. Security Deepest level of security New security threats drive the need for new protections. HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection5, exclusively from HP, identifies and fixes BIOS attacks and Windows 10 Pro2 allows multi-factor authentication to help secure access to business networks and resources. IR camera Leave passwords behind. Use Windows Hello biometric authentication with the IR camera to help prevent unauthorized access to business networks and resources with Windows 10 Pro.2 Screens simulate, subject to change; Apps sold separately, availability may vary. Performance Performance to get the job done The HP EliteBook Folio handles high-performance requirements with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processor,6 PCle SSDs, 8GB of memory, and long battery life. Clarity Clear, sharp vivid display Choose a crystal-clear UHD display3 with four times more pixels than FHD displays for color critical applications, or an FHD touch display3 for outstanding visual and touch interactivity. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. With hand-selected materials and premium features optimized for collaboration, it's the choice for those who value a flawless experience. View all options Elevating durable design Cutting-edge design, innovative engineering, and refined materials come together in the sophisticated and durable HP EliteBook Folio. Equipped to get the job done Be productive in any situation. Windows 10 Pro2 and powerful security, collaboration, and connectivity features from HP help you power through your day on the HP EliteBook Folio. Windows Hello biometric authentication with IR camera HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard Bang & Olufsen audio 12.5 diagonal inch UHD touchscreen3 Dock capable (via USB Type-C™ ports with Thunderbolt™) Premium collaboration Engage teams, clients, and vendors with the crystal-clear audio by Bang & Olufsen and the high-performance HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard that allows you to launch calls and video chats at the touch of a button on the world's first notebook purpose-built for collaboration.4 The solution for diverse business demands Design Elevating exceptional design Weighing less than 2.2 lb/1kg this PC is designed to turn heads with a polished diamond-cut CNC aluminum, durable body. The ultra-thin design features a 180-degree unique piano hinge to lay completely flat for easy sharing with others. Security Deepest level of security New security threats drive the need for new protections. HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection5, exclusively from HP, identifies and fixes BIOS attacks and Windows 10 Pro2 allows multi-factor authentication to help secure access to business networks and resources. IR camera Leave passwords behind. Use Windows Hello biometric authentication with the IR camera to help prevent unauthorized access to business networks and resources with Windows 10 Pro.2 Screens simulate, subject to change; Apps sold separately, availability may vary. Performance Performance to get the job done The HP EliteBook Folio handles high-performance requirements with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processor,6 PCle SSDs, 8GB of memory, and long battery life. Clarity Clear, sharp vivid display Choose a crystal-clear UHD display3 with four times more pixels than FHD displays for color critical applications, or an FHD touch display3 for outstanding visual and touch interactivity. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. To top Features Buy Back Features HP EliteBook Folio HP EliteBook Folio The world's thinnest and lightest business-class notebook.1 Exquisite craftsmanship and exceptional performance are united in the HP EliteBook Folio. With hand-selected materials and premium features optimized for collaboration, it's the choice for those who value a flawless experience. View all options Elevating durable design Cutting-edge design, innovative engineering, and refined materials come together in the sophisticated and durable HP EliteBook Folio. Equipped to get the job done Be productive in any situation. Windows 10 Pro2 and powerful security, collaboration, and connectivity features from HP help you power through your day on the HP EliteBook Folio. Windows Hello biometric authentication with IR camera HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard Bang & Olufsen audio 12.5 diagonal inch UHD touchscreen3 Dock capable (via USB Type-C™ ports with Thunderbolt™) Premium collaboration Engage teams, clients, and vendors with the crystal-clear audio by Bang & Olufsen and the high-performance HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard that allows you to launch calls and video chats at the touch of a button on the world's first notebook purpose-built for collaboration.4 The solution for diverse business demands Design Elevating exceptional design Weighing less than 2.2 lb/1kg this PC is designed to turn heads with a polished diamond-cut CNC aluminum, durable body. The ultra-thin design features a 180-degree unique piano hinge to lay completely flat for easy sharing with others. Security Deepest level of security New security threats drive the need for new protections. HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection5, exclusively from HP, identifies and fixes BIOS attacks and Windows 10 Pro2 allows multi-factor authentication to help secure access to business networks and resources. IR camera Leave passwords behind. Use Windows Hello biometric authentication with the IR camera to help prevent unauthorized access to business networks and resources with Windows 10 Pro.2 Screens simulate, subject to change; Apps sold separately, availability may vary. Performance Performance to get the job done The HP EliteBook Folio handles high-performance requirements with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processor,6 PCle SSDs, 8GB of memory, and long battery life. Clarity Clear, sharp vivid display Choose a crystal-clear UHD display3 with four times more pixels than FHD displays for color critical applications, or an FHD touch display3 for outstanding visual and touch interactivity. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. Back Features HP EliteBook Folio HP EliteBook Folio The world's thinnest and lightest business-class notebook.1 Exquisite craftsmanship and exceptional performance are united in the HP EliteBook Folio. With hand-selected materials and premium features optimized for collaboration, it's the choice for those who value a flawless experience. View all options Elevating durable design Cutting-edge design, innovative engineering, and refined materials come together in the sophisticated and durable HP EliteBook Folio. Equipped to get the job done Be productive in any situation. Windows 10 Pro2 and powerful security, collaboration, and connectivity features from HP help you power through your day on the HP EliteBook Folio. Windows Hello biometric authentication with IR camera HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard Bang & Olufsen audio 12.5 diagonal inch UHD touchscreen3 Dock capable (via USB Type-C™ ports with Thunderbolt™) Premium collaboration Engage teams, clients, and vendors with the crystal-clear audio by Bang & Olufsen and the high-performance HP Premium Collaboration Keyboard that allows you to launch calls and video chats at the touch of a button on the world's first notebook purpose-built for collaboration.4 The solution for diverse business demands Design Elevating exceptional design Weighing less than 2.2 lb/1kg this PC is designed to turn heads with a polished diamond-cut CNC aluminum, durable body. The ultra-thin design features a 180-degree unique piano hinge to lay completely flat for easy sharing with others. Security Deepest level of security New security threats drive the need for new protections. HP Sure Start with Dynamic Protection5, exclusively from HP, identifies and fixes BIOS attacks and Windows 10 Pro2 allows multi-factor authentication to help secure access to business networks and resources. IR camera Leave passwords behind. Use Windows Hello biometric authentication with the IR camera to help prevent unauthorized access to business networks and resources with Windows 10 Pro.2 Screens simulate, subject to change; Apps sold separately, availability may vary. Performance Performance to get the job done The HP EliteBook Folio handles high-performance requirements with a 6th Gen Intel® Core™ processor,6 PCle SSDs, 8GB of memory, and long battery life. Clarity Clear, sharp vivid display Choose a crystal-clear UHD display3 with four times more pixels than FHD displays for color critical applications, or an FHD touch display3 for outstanding visual and touch interactivity. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit. Extreme tests for extreme dependability7 The HP EliteBook Folio has passed MIL-STD 810G tests7. Add another 120,000 hours of our own testing and end-to-end diagnostics, and you get confidence built right in. Movement We simulated the vibrations of 1000 miles of ground transportation and jolted the laptop in six directions for a total of 18 mechanical shocks. Dust Test Our laptop was dusted with Arizona road dust for six hours while being operated to ensure components won't fail in harsh environments. Drop Test We made 26 drops from 30 inches onto every side, angle and edge onto 2 inches of plywood over steel and concrete to ensure toughness. Environmental We subject the laptop to a simulated altitude pressure of 15,000 feet. Then, it is exposed to a temperature change of more than 212° Fahrenheit.
